## Instruction

You need to read the inventory levels of WooCommerce products, check the current stock quantity (stock_quantity) for each product against the safety threshold (stock_threshold), identify all products with stock below the threshold, and automatically update a Google Sheets purchase requisition list named stock_sheet. For each low-stock product, record it in Google Sheets and send an email notification to the purchasing manager (the email address is in purchasing_manager_email.txt). You need to find all low-stock products, record them and send emails. The email template can be found in stock_alert_email_template.md.

### WooCommerce

You can review the data construction process during testing [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/woocommerce-stock-alert/preprocess).

```json output_result
# Stock Alert Email Template

## Email Subject
[Stock Alert] {product_name} Stock Below Safety Threshold

## Email Body

Dear Purchasing Manager,

The system has detected that the following product's stock level is below the safety threshold. Please take immediate action:

## Product Information
- **Product Name**: {product_name}
- **SKU**: {sku}
- **Current Stock**: {current_stock}
- **Safety Threshold**: {threshold}
- **Supplier**: {supplier_name}
- **Supplier Contact**: {supplier_contact}

## Action Required
Please review the stock levels and consider placing a purchase order to replenish inventory.

For detailed information and to update the purchase requisition list, please visit the Google Sheets link: {google_sheets_link}

Best regards,
Stock Alert System
```

```python
            {"key": "category", "value": "Electronics"}
        ]
    },

        "id": 9,
        "name": "Laptop Dell XPS 13",
        "sku": "DELL-XPS-13",
        "stock_quantity": 5,
        "meta_data": [
            {"key": "stock_threshold", "value": "10"},
            {"key": "supplier", "value": {"name": "Dell China", "contact": "supplier@dell.cn", "supplier_id": "SUP001"}},
            {"key": "category", "value": "Electronics"}
        ]
    }
]

all_products = products_page1 + products_page2

# Function to extract metadata value
def get_meta_value(meta_data, key):
    for item in meta_data:
        if item["key"] == key:
            return item["value"]
    return None

# Identify low-stock products
low_stock_products = []

for product in all_products:
    stock_quantity = product["stock_quantity"]
    stock_threshold = int(get_meta_value(product["meta_data"], "stock_threshold"))
    supplier_info = get_meta_value(product["meta_data"], "supplier")
    category = get_meta_value(product["meta_data"], "category")
    
    if stock_quantity < stock_threshold:
        low_stock_products.append({
            "id": product["id"],
            "name": product["name"],
            "sku": product["sku"],
            "current_stock": stock_quantity,
            "threshold": stock_threshold,
            "supplier_name": supplier_info["name"],
            "supplier_contact": supplier_info["contact"],
            "category": category
        })

print("Low Stock Products Found:")
print("=" * 50)
for product in low_stock_products:
    print(f"Product: {product['name']}")
    print(f"SKU: {product['sku']}")
    print(f"Current Stock: {product['current_stock']}")
    print(f"Threshold: {product['threshold']}")
    print(f"Supplier: {product['supplier_name']} ({product['supplier_contact']})")
    print(f"Category: {product['category']}")
    print("-" * 30)

print(f"\nTotal low-stock products: {len(low_stock_products)}") code
```

```python
# Get current timestamp
current_time = datetime.now().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")

# Prepare data for Google Sheets (starting from row 2, since row 1 has headers)
sheet_data = []

for product in low_stock_products:
    # Calculate suggested order quantity (threshold * 2 - current_stock)
    suggested_qty = max(product["threshold"] * 2 - product["current_stock"], product["threshold"])
    
    row = [
        str(product["id"]),
        product["name"],
        product["sku"],
        product["current_stock"],
        str(product["threshold"]),
        product["supplier_name"],
        product["supplier_id"],
        product["supplier_contact"],
        current_time,
        str(suggested_qty)
    ]
    sheet_data.append(row)

print("Data prepared for Google Sheets:")
print("=" * 50)
for i, row in enumerate(sheet_data):
    print(f"Row {i+2}: {row}")

print(f"\nTotal rows to add: {len(sheet_data)}")
print(f"Range will be: A2:J{len(sheet_data)+1}") code
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```python
# Email template from the file
email_template = """Dear Purchasing Manager,

The system has detected that the following product's stock level is below the safety threshold. Please take immediate action:

## Product Information
- **Product Name**: {product_name}
- **SKU**: {sku}
- **Current Stock**: {current_stock}
- **Safety Threshold**: {threshold}
- **Supplier**: {supplier_name}
- **Supplier Contact**: {supplier_contact}

## Action Required
Please review the stock levels and consider placing a purchase order to replenish inventory.

For detailed information and to update the purchase requisition list, please visit the Google Sheets link: https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1qrXcYzdRsoLaEzEiQqEbFhkFQGD8JGOXUGPT2XYdFG8

Best regards,
Stock Alert System"""

# Purchasing manager email
purchasing_manager_email = "laura_thompson@mcp.com"

# Generate email content for each low-stock product
emails_to_send = []

for product in low_stock_products:
    subject = f"[Stock Alert] {product['name']} Stock Below Safety Threshold"
    
    body = email_template.format(
        product_name=product['name'],
        sku=product['sku'],
        current_stock=product['current_stock'],
        threshold=product['threshold'],
        supplier_name=product['supplier_name'],
        supplier_contact=product['supplier_contact'],
        google_sheets_link="https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1qrXcYzdRsoLaEzEiQqEbFhkFQGD8JGOXUGPT2XYdFG8"
    )
    
    emails_to_send.append({
        'subject': subject,
        'body': body,
        'product_name': product['name']
    })

print(f"Prepared {len(emails_to_send)} emails to send to {purchasing_manager_email}")
print("\nEmail subjects:")
for i, email in enumerate(emails_to_send):
    print(f"{i+1}. {email['subject']}") code
```

```python
        sku=product['sku'],
        current_stock=product['current_stock'],
        threshold=product['threshold'],
        supplier_name=product['supplier_name'],
        supplier_contact=product['supplier_contact'],
        google_sheets_link="https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1qrXcYzdRsoLaEzEiQqEbFhkFQGD8JGOXUGPT2XYdFG8"
    )
    
    emails_to_send.append({
        'subject': subject,
        'body': body,
        'product_name': product['name']
    })

print(f"Prepared {len(emails_to_send)} emails to send to {purchasing_manager_email}")
print("\nEmail subjects:")
for i, email in enumerate(emails_to_send):
    print(f"{i+1}. {email['subject']}") code
```

```python
print("=" * 60)
print("INVENTORY MONITORING TASK COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY")
print("=" * 60)

print("\n📊 INVENTORY ANALYSIS RESULTS:")
print("-" * 40)
print(f"Total products analyzed: 13")
print(f"Products below safety threshold: 8")
print(f"Products with adequate stock: 5")

print("\n🚨 LOW-STOCK PRODUCTS IDENTIFIED:")
print("-" * 40)
low_stock_summary = [
    ("Nintendo Switch OLED", "NINTENDO-SWITCH-OLED", 2, 12, "Critical"),
    ("MacBook Pro 14-inch M3", "MACBOOK-PRO-14-M3", 3, 8, "Low"),
    ("Microsoft Surface Pro 9", "MS-SURFACE-PRO9", 1, 6, "Critical"),
    ("Canon EOS R6", "CANON-EOS-R6", 4, 8, "Low"),
    ("iPad Air 5th Gen", "IPAD-AIR-5", 7, 12, "Low"),
    ("Samsung 65\" QLED TV", "SAMSUNG-Q80B-65", 2, 5, "Low"),
    ("iPhone 15 Pro", "IPHONE-15-PRO", 3, 15, "Critical"),
    ("Laptop Dell XPS 13", "DELL-XPS-13", 5, 10, "Low")
]

for i, (name, sku, stock, threshold, priority) in enumerate(low_stock_summary, 1):
    print(f"{i}. {name}")
    print(f"   SKU: {sku}")
    print(f"   Stock: {stock} (Threshold: {threshold}) - Priority: {priority}")
    print()

print("\n📋 GOOGLE SHEETS UPDATED:")
print("-" * 40)
print("✅ Purchase requisition list updated with all 8 low-stock products")
print("✅ Added product details, supplier information, and suggested order quantities")
print("✅ Timestamp recorded for tracking purposes")
print("📄 Google Sheets URL: https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1qrXcYzdRsoLaEzEiQqEbFhkFQGD8JGOXUGPT2XYdFG8")

print("\n📧 EMAIL NOTIFICATIONS SENT:")
print("-" * 40)
print("✅ 8 individual stock alert emails sent to purchasing manager")
print("✅ Recipient: laura_thompson@mcp.com")
print("✅ Each email contains specific product details and supplier contact information")
print("✅ All emails include link to the updated Google Sheets")

print("\n🎯 NEXT STEPS FOR PURCHASING MANAGER:")
print("-" * 40)
print("1. Review the Google Sheets purchase requisition list")
print("2. Contact suppliers for the critical priority items first:")
print("   - Nintendo Switch OLED (only 2 left, need 22)")
print("   - Microsoft Surface Pro 9 (only 1 left, need 11)")
print("   - iPhone 15 Pro (only 3 left, need 27)")
print("3. Place purchase orders based on suggested quantities")
print("4. Update order status in the Google Sheets")

print("\n" + "=" * 60) code
```

```python
import datetime

now = datetime.datetime.now().isoformat()

low_stock_products = [
    {
        "id": 18,
        "name": "Nintendo Switch OLED",
        "sku": "NINTENDO-SWITCH-OLED",
        "stock_quantity": 2,
        "stock_threshold": 12,
        "supplier": "Nintendo Distribution",
        "supplier_id": "SUP009",
        "supplier_contact": "orders@nintendo-dist.com"
    },
    {
        "id": 17,
        "name": "MacBook Pro 14-inch M3",
        "sku": "MACBOOK-PRO-14-M3",
        "stock_quantity": 3,
        "stock_threshold": 8,
        "supplier": "Apple Corporate Sales",
        "supplier_id": "SUP008",
        "supplier_contact": "corporate@apple.com"
    },
    {
        "id": 16,
        "name": "Microsoft Surface Pro 9",
        "sku": "MS-SURFACE-PRO9",
        "stock_quantity": 1,
        "stock_threshold": 6,
        "supplier": "Microsoft China",
        "supplier_id": "SUP007",
        "supplier_contact": "surface@microsoft.cn"
    },
    {
        "id": 15,
        "name": "Canon EOS R6",
        "sku": "CANON-EOS-R6",
        "stock_quantity": 4,
        "stock_threshold": 8,
        "supplier": "Canon Professional",
        "supplier_id": "SUP006",
        "supplier_contact": "pro@canon.com.cn"
    },
    {
        "id": 14,
        "name": "iPad Air 5th Gen",
        "sku": "IPAD-AIR-5",
        "stock_quantity": 7,
        "stock_threshold": 12,
        "supplier": "Apple Authorized Distributor",
        "supplier_id": "SUP002",
        "supplier_contact": "sales@apple-distributor.cn"
    },
    {
        "id": 12,
        "name": "Samsung 65\" QLED TV",
        "sku": "SAMSUNG-Q80B-65",
        "stock_quantity": 2,
        "stock_threshold": 5,
        "supplier": "Samsung Display",
        "supplier_id": "SUP004",
        "supplier_contact": "b2b@samsung.cn"
    }
]

data_to_write = []
for product in low_stock_products:
    suggested_quantity = product["stock_threshold"] - product["stock_quantity"]
    data_to_write.append([
        product["id"],
        product["name"],
        product["sku"],
        product["stock_quantity"],
        product["stock_threshold"],
        product["supplier"],
        product["supplier_id"],
        product["supplier_contact"],
        now,
        suggested_quantity
    ])

print(data_to_write)
```
